## 5ï¸âƒ£ CODE SKELETON MáºªU (Java)

### **Server - AuctionServer.java (ÄÆ¡n giáº£n nháº¥t):**

```java
import java.io.*;
import java.net.*;
import java.util.*;

public class AuctionServer {
    private static final int PORT = 8888;
    private static List<ClientHandler> clients = new ArrayList<>();
    private static double currentPrice = 100.0;
    private static String highestBidder = "None";
    
    public static void main(String[] args) throws IOException {
        ServerSocket serverSocket = new ServerSocket(PORT);
        System.out.println("Server started on port " + PORT);
        
        while (true) {
            Socket clientSocket = serverSocket.accept();
            ClientHandler handler = new ClientHandler(clientSocket);
            clients.add(handler);
            new Thread(handler).start();
        }
    }
    
    public static synchronized void broadcastBid(String bidder, double amount) {
        currentPrice = amount;
        highestBidder = bidder;
        String message = "BID_UPDATE|" + bidder + "|" + amount;
        
        for (ClientHandler client : clients) {
            client.sendMessage(message);
        }
    }
}
```

### **Client - AuctionClient.java (ÄÆ¡n giáº£n):**

```java
import java.io.*;
import java.net.*;

public class AuctionClient {
    private Socket socket;
    private PrintWriter out;
    private BufferedReader in;
    
    public void connect(String host, int port) throws IOException {
        socket = new Socket(host, port);
        out = new PrintWriter(socket.getOutputStream(), true);
        in = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(socket.getInputStream()));
        
        // Thread nháº­n messages tá»« server
        new Thread(() -> {
            try {
                String message;
                while ((message = in.readLine()) != null) {
                    handleServerMessage(message);
                }
            } catch (IOException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
        }).start();
    }
    
    public void placeBid(String username, double amount) {
        out.println("BID|" + username + "|" + amount);
    }
    
    private void handleServerMessage(String message) {
        // Parse vÃ  update GUI
        System.out.println("Received: " + message);
    }
}
```

## 6ï¸âƒ£ ÄIá»‚M Ná»”I Báº¬T Vá»€ Láº¬P TRÃŒNH Máº NG (NÃªu trong presentation)

Khi thuyáº¿t trÃ¬nh, nháº¥n máº¡nh cÃ¡c khÃ­a cáº¡nh network programming:

âœ… **Socket Programming:**
- TCP connection giá»¯a client-server
- `ServerSocket` accept multiple connections
- `Socket` send/receive data streams

âœ… **Multi-threading:**
- Thread per client (ClientHandler)
- Synchronization cho shared data (currentPrice)
- Thread-safe broadcast

âœ… **Protocol Design:**
- Custom text-based protocol
- Message format: `COMMAND|param1|param2`
- Error handling

âœ… **Real-time Communication:**
- Push-based updates (server â†’ clients)
- Low latency requirements
- State synchronization

âœ… **Concurrency Issues:**
- Race condition khi 2 ngÆ°á»i bid cÃ¹ng lÃºc
- Giáº£i phÃ¡p: `synchronized` methods
- Atomic operations

```java
public class AuctionServer {
    private static final int PORT = 8888;
    private static List<ClientHandler> clients = new ArrayList<>();
    private static double currentPrice = 100.0;
    private static String highestBidder = "None";
    
    public static void main(String[] args) throws IOException {
        ServerSocket serverSocket = new ServerSocket(PORT);
        System.out.println("Server started on port " + PORT);
        
        while (true) {
            Socket clientSocket = serverSocket.accept();
            ClientHandler handler = new ClientHandler(clientSocket);
            clients.add(handler);
            new Thread(handler).start();
        }
    }
    
    public static synchronized void broadcastBid(String bidder, double amount) {
        currentPrice = amount;
        highestBidder = bidder;
        String message = "BID_UPDATE|" + bidder + "|" + amount;
        
        for (ClientHandler client : clients) {
            client.sendMessage(message);
        }
    }
}
```

```java
import java.io.*;
import java.net.*;

public class AuctionClient {
    private Socket socket;
    private PrintWriter out;
    private BufferedReader in;
    
    public void connect(String host, int port) throws IOException {
        socket = new Socket(host, port);
        out = new PrintWriter(socket.getOutputStream(), true);
        in = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(socket.getInputStream()));
        
        // Thread nháº­n messages tá»« server
        new Thread(() -> {
            try {
                String message;
                while ((message = in.readLine()) != null) {
                    handleServerMessage(message);
                }
            } catch (IOException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
        }).start();
    }
    
    public void placeBid(String username, double amount) {
        out.println("BID|" + username + "|" + amount);
    }
    
    private void handleServerMessage(String message) {
        // Parse vÃ  update GUI
        System.out.println("Received: " + message);
    }
}
```

### **B. CÃ”NG NGHá»† SERVER**

#### **1. Socket Programming - TCP/IP**

**Chi tiáº¿t ká»¹ thuáº­t:**

- **LÃ½ do khÃ´ng dÃ¹ng UDP:**

  - Quan trá»ng cho Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡ (khÃ´ng thá»ƒ máº¥t bid)

**Cá»•ng sá»­ dá»¥ng:**

#### **2. Multi-threading**

**MÃ´ hÃ¬nh threading:**

#### **3. Synchronization (Äá»“ng bá»™ hÃ³a)**
```
ğŸ“¦ Package: java.util.concurrent
- ConcurrentHashMap: Map thread-safe

- AtomicInteger/AtomicLong: Biáº¿n atomic

```

**VÃ­ dá»¥ váº¥n Ä‘á» cáº§n giáº£i quyáº¿t:**

```
â””â”€â”€ âŒ Káº¾T QUáº¢: Cáº£ 2 Ä‘á»u Ä‘Æ°á»£c cháº¥p nháº­n (SAI!)

â”œâ”€â”€ Server lock â†’ xá»­ lÃ½ bid Alice: 25tr âœ…

â””â”€â”€ âœ… Káº¾T QUáº¢: Chá»‰ Alice tháº¯ng (ÄÃšNG!)
```

### **D. CÆ  Sá» Dá»® LIá»†U**

#### **SQLite (Khuyáº¿n nghá»‹ cho Má»©c 3)**

**LÃ½ do chá»n SQLite:**
- âœ… Nháº¹, khÃ´ng cáº§n cÃ i Ä‘áº·t server riÃªng
- âœ… Dá»… setup, chá»‰ cáº§n 1 file .db
- âœ… Äá»§ cho demo vÃ  presentation
- âœ… Há»— trá»£ SQL Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§

**ThÆ° viá»‡n:**

**Alternative: MySQL** (náº¿u muá»‘n professional hÆ¡n)

```
ğŸ“¦ MySQL Connector/J

- Cáº§n cÃ i MySQL Server riÃªng
```

#### **Schema Database (Má»©c 3):**

```sql
-- Báº£ng Users (NgÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng)
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    username VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    balance DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1
);

-- Báº£ng Auctions (CÃ¡c phiÃªn Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡)
CREATE TABLE auctions (
    auction_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    item_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    starting_price DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    current_price DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    reserve_price DECIMAL(15,2),  -- GiÃ¡ dá»± trá»¯
    highest_bidder_id INTEGER,
    start_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'ACTIVE',  -- ACTIVE, ENDED, CANCELLED
    bid_increment DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 500000,  -- BÆ°á»›c nháº£y giÃ¡
    created_by INTEGER,
    FOREIGN KEY (highest_bidder_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (created_by) REFERENCES users(user_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Bids (Lá»‹ch sá»­ Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡)
CREATE TABLE bids (
    bid_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    auction_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    bid_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    bid_time TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_auto_bid BOOLEAN DEFAULT 0,  -- Bid tá»± Ä‘á»™ng hay khÃ´ng
    FOREIGN KEY (auction_id) REFERENCES auctions(auction_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Auto_Bids (Äáº¥u giÃ¡ tá»± Ä‘á»™ng)
CREATE TABLE auto_bids (
    auto_bid_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    auction_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    max_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,  -- GiÃ¡ tá»‘i Ä‘a
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (auction_id) REFERENCES auctions(auction_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Watchlist (Theo dÃµi)
CREATE TABLE watchlist (
    watchlist_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    auction_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    added_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (auction_id) REFERENCES auctions(auction_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Admin_Logs (Nháº­t kÃ½ quáº£n trá»‹)
CREATE TABLE admin_logs (
    log_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    admin_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    action VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    details TEXT,
    timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (admin_id) REFERENCES users(user_id)
);
```

## 2ï¸âƒ£ GIAO THá»¨C NETWORK (CUSTOM PROTOCOL)

### **A. THIáº¾T Káº¾ GIAO THá»¨C**

#### **Loáº¡i giao thá»©c: Text-based Protocol over TCP**

**Format cÆ¡ báº£n:**
```
COMMAND|param1|param2|param3|...
```

**LÃ½ do chá»n text-based:**
- âœ… Dá»… debug (cÃ³ thá»ƒ Ä‘á»c Ä‘Æ°á»£c)
- âœ… Dá»… implement
- âœ… Dá»… má»Ÿ rá»™ng
- âœ… Äá»§ nhanh cho Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡ (< 100ms latency)

**Alternative:** Binary protocol (nhanh hÆ¡n nhÆ°ng phá»©c táº¡p hÆ¡n)

---

### **B. CÃC LOáº I MESSAGES**

#### **1. Authentication Messages (XÃ¡c thá»±c)**

**Client â†’ Server:**
```
REGISTER|username|password|email
LOGIN|username|password
LOGOUT
```

**Server â†’ Client:**
```
AUTH_SUCCESS|user_id|username|balance
AUTH_FAILED|error_message
REGISTER_SUCCESS|user_id
REGISTER_FAILED|error_message
```

**VÃ­ dá»¥ thá»±c táº¿:**
```
Client gá»­i: LOGIN|alice|mypassword123
Server tráº£:  AUTH_SUCCESS|101|alice|50000000.00
```

---

#### **2. Auction Listing Messages (Danh sÃ¡ch Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡)**

**Client â†’ Server:**
```
LIST_AUCTIONS                    // Láº¥y táº¥t cáº£
LIST_AUCTIONS|ACTIVE             // Chá»‰ Ä‘ang diá»…n ra
LIST_AUCTIONS|MY_BIDS            // Nhá»¯ng cÃ¡i tÃ´i Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘áº¥u
LIST_AUCTIONS|SEARCH|keyword     // TÃ¬m kiáº¿m
```

**Server â†’ Client:**
```

Format cá»§a auction_data:
id:name:currentPrice:highestBidder:timeLeft:status

VÃ­ dá»¥:
AUCTION_LIST|3|1:iPhone:25000000:Bob:154:ACTIVE|2:MacBook:35000000:Alice:320:ACTIVE
```

---

#### **3. Auction Detail Messages (Chi tiáº¿t Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡)**

**Client â†’ Server:**
```

```

**Server â†’ Client:**
```

BID_HISTORY|count|bid1_data|bid2_data|...
Format: bidder:amount:timestamp

VÃ­ dá»¥:
BID_HISTORY|3|Bob:25000000:2025-10-28T14:30:25|Alice:24000000:2025-10-28T14:29:10
```

---

#### **4. Bidding Messages (Äáº·t giÃ¡)**

**Client â†’ Server:**
```

```

**Server â†’ Client:**
```

BID_FAILED|auction_id|reason

Reasons:
- PRICE_TOO_LOW: GiÃ¡ tháº¥p hÆ¡n giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i
- INSUFFICIENT_FUNDS: KhÃ´ng Ä‘á»§ tiá»n
- AUCTION_ENDED: Äáº¥u giÃ¡ Ä‘Ã£ káº¿t thÃºc
- SELF_HIGHEST: Báº¡n Ä‘ang dáº«n Ä‘áº§u rá»“i
- INVALID_INCREMENT: KhÃ´ng Ä‘Ãºng bÆ°á»›c nháº£y
```

---

#### **5. Real-time Update Messages (Cáº­p nháº­t thá»i gian thá»±c)**

**Server â†’ All Clients in Auction:**
```
BID_UPDATE|auction_id|bidder_username|new_price|time_left
OUTBID_ALERT|auction_id|new_price|new_bidder
AUCTION_EXTENDED|auction_id|new_end_time|reason
AUCTION_ENDING_SOON|auction_id|seconds_left
AUCTION_ENDED|auction_id|winner_username|final_price|total_bids
TIME_TICK|auction_id|seconds_left
```

**VÃ­ dá»¥ flow:**
```
1. Bob Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡ 25tr:
   Server â†’ All: BID_UPDATE|1|Bob|25000000|145

2. Alice bá»‹ Ä‘Ã¨ giÃ¡:
   Server â†’ Alice: OUTBID_ALERT|1|25000000|Bob

3. Ai Ä‘Ã³ Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡ trong 10s cuá»‘i:
   Server â†’ All: AUCTION_EXTENDED|1|2025-10-28T15:05:00|LATE_BID

4. Äáº¿m ngÆ°á»£c:
   Server â†’ All: TIME_TICK|1|30
   Server â†’ All: TIME_TICK|1|29
   ...

5. Káº¿t thÃºc:
   Server â†’ All: AUCTION_ENDED|1|Bob|30000000|15
```

### **C. HEARTBEAT MECHANISM (CÆ¡ cháº¿ nhá»‹p tim)**

**Má»¥c Ä‘Ã­ch:** PhÃ¡t hiá»‡n káº¿t ná»‘i cháº¿t (dead connection)

**CÆ¡ cháº¿:**
```
Má»—i 30 giÃ¢y:
â”œâ”€â”€ Server gá»­i: PING
â”œâ”€â”€ Client pháº£i tráº£ lá»i trong 5s: PONG
â””â”€â”€ Náº¿u khÃ´ng tráº£ lá»i: Server ngáº¯t káº¿t ná»‘i
```

**Implementation:**
```java
// Server side
ScheduledExecutorService heartbeat = Executors.newScheduledThreadPool(1);
heartbeat.scheduleAtFixedRate(() -> {
    for (ClientHandler client : clients) {
        if (!client.isAlive()) {
            client.disconnect();
        } else {
            client.sendPing();
        }
    }
}, 0, 30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
```

---

### **D. MESSAGE ENCODING & SECURITY**

#### **1. Encoding:**
```
Character Set: UTF-8
Line Terminator: \n (newline)
Delimiter: | (pipe)
```

#### **2. Escaping (Xá»­ lÃ½ kÃ½ tá»± Ä‘áº·c biá»‡t):**
```
Náº¿u data chá»©a |: thay báº±ng \|
Náº¿u data chá»©a \: thay báº±ng \\
Náº¿u data chá»©a \n: thay báº±ng \n
```

#### **3. Basic Security (Má»©c 3):**

**Máº­t kháº©u:**
```java
// KhÃ´ng lÆ°u plain text
// DÃ¹ng BCrypt hash
import org.mindrot.jbcrypt.BCrypt;

String hashed = BCrypt.hashpw(plainPassword, BCrypt.gensalt(12));
boolean match = BCrypt.checkpw(plainPassword, hashedPassword);
```

**SSL/TLS (Optional nhÆ°ng nÃªn cÃ³):**
```java
// DÃ¹ng SSLSocket thay vÃ¬ Socket thÃ´ng thÆ°á»ng
SSLSocketFactory factory = (SSLSocketFactory) SSLSocketFactory.getDefault();
SSLSocket sslSocket = (SSLSocket) factory.createSocket(host, port);
```

## 4ï¸âƒ£ KIáº¾N TRÃšC Há»† THá»NG

### **Architecture Overview:**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚                    SERVER SIDE                          â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  Main Server Thread                               â”‚  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  - Khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng ServerSocket                        â”‚  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  - Accept connections                             â”‚  â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  - Khá»Ÿi táº¡o Database                             â”‚  â”‚
```

```sql
-- Báº£ng Users (NgÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng)
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    username VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    balance DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1
);

-- Báº£ng Auctions (CÃ¡c phiÃªn Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡)
CREATE TABLE auctions (
    auction_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    item_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    starting_price DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    current_price DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    reserve_price DECIMAL(15,2),  -- GiÃ¡ dá»± trá»¯
    highest_bidder_id INTEGER,
    start_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'ACTIVE',  -- ACTIVE, ENDED, CANCELLED
    bid_increment DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 500000,  -- BÆ°á»›c nháº£y giÃ¡
    created_by INTEGER,
    FOREIGN KEY (highest_bidder_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (created_by) REFERENCES users(user_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Bids (Lá»‹ch sá»­ Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡)
CREATE TABLE bids (
    bid_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    auction_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    bid_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,
    bid_time TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_auto_bid BOOLEAN DEFAULT 0,  -- Bid tá»± Ä‘á»™ng hay khÃ´ng
    FOREIGN KEY (auction_id) REFERENCES auctions(auction_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Auto_Bids (Äáº¥u giÃ¡ tá»± Ä‘á»™ng)
CREATE TABLE auto_bids (
    auto_bid_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    auction_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    max_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,  -- GiÃ¡ tá»‘i Ä‘a
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT 1,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (auction_id) REFERENCES auctions(auction_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Watchlist (Theo dÃµi)
CREATE TABLE watchlist (
    watchlist_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    auction_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    added_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (auction_id) REFERENCES auctions(auction_id)
);

-- Báº£ng Admin_Logs (Nháº­t kÃ½ quáº£n trá»‹)
CREATE TABLE admin_logs (
    log_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    admin_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    action VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    details TEXT,
    timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (admin_id) REFERENCES users(user_id)
);
```

```java
// Server side
ScheduledExecutorService heartbeat = Executors.newScheduledThreadPool(1);
heartbeat.scheduleAtFixedRate(() -> {
    for (ClientHandler client : clients) {
        if (!client.isAlive()) {
            client.disconnect();
        } else {
            client.sendPing();
        }
    }
}, 0, 30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
```

## ğŸ”§ CÃ”NG NGHá»† CHI TIáº¾T

### **1. MySQL Schema:**
```
Database: auction_db
Tables: 6 tables (nhÆ° Ä‘Ã£ nÃ³i á»Ÿ trÃªn)
Storage Engine: InnoDB
Charset: utf8mb4
Collation: utf8mb4_unicode_ci
```

### **2. Network Protocol:**
```
Transport: TCP/IP
Format: Text-based (delimiter: |)
Encoding: UTF-8
Heartbeat: 30s interval
Commands: 30+ message types
```

### **3. Threading Model:**
```
Main Thread: Accept connections
Thread Pool: 50 worker threads
Timer Pool: Per-auction countdown threads
Synchronization: synchronized + ConcurrentHashMap
```

### **4. Security:**
```
Password: BCrypt (cost factor 12)
Connection: Optional SSL/TLS
Validation: Server-side input validation
SQL Injection: PreparedStatement
```

### **5. JavaFX UI Components:**
```
- TableView: Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ danh sÃ¡ch auctions
- ListView: Bid history
- ProgressBar: Countdown timer
- TextField: Input fields
- Button: Actions
- Alert: Notifications
- LineChart: Price history graph
- TabPane: Multiple views
```

## 5ï¸âƒ£ DATABASE SCHEMA

### **Báº£ng 1: users (NgÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng)**
```
Columns:
- user_id (INT, PK, AUTO_INCREMENT)
- username (VARCHAR(50), UNIQUE, NOT NULL)
- email (VARCHAR(100), UNIQUE, NOT NULL)
- password_hash (VARCHAR(255), NOT NULL)
- full_name (VARCHAR(100))
- balance (DECIMAL(15,2), DEFAULT 0)
- role (ENUM('USER', 'ADMIN'), DEFAULT 'USER')
- is_active (BOOLEAN, DEFAULT TRUE)
- created_at (TIMESTAMP, DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
```


### **C. Bidding APIs**

### **D. Watchlist APIs**

### **E. User APIs**

## 7ï¸âƒ£ WEBSOCKET MESSAGES

### **Client â†’ Server**
```javascript
// Äáº·t giÃ¡
{
  type: "PLACE_BID",
  auctionId: 1,
  amount: 25000000
}

// Join auction room
{
  type: "JOIN_AUCTION",
  auctionId: 1
}

// Leave auction room
{
  type: "LEAVE_AUCTION",
  auctionId: 1
}
```

### **Server â†’ Client**
```javascript
// Cáº­p nháº­t giÃ¡ má»›i
{
  type: "BID_UPDATE",
  auctionId: 1,
  bidderName: "Bob",
  newPrice: 25000000,
  timeLeft: 145
}

// Báº¡n bá»‹ Ä‘Ã¨ giÃ¡
{
  type: "OUTBID_ALERT",
  auctionId: 1,
  newPrice: 26000000,
  newBidder: "Alice"
}

// Countdown tick
{
  type: "TIME_TICK",
  auctionId: 1,
  secondsLeft: 30
}

// Auction sáº¯p káº¿t thÃºc
{
  type: "AUCTION_ENDING_SOON",
  auctionId: 1,
  secondsLeft: 60
}

// Auction gia háº¡n
{
  type: "AUCTION_EXTENDED",
  auctionId: 1,
  newEndTime: "2025-10-28T15:05:00",
  reason: "Late bid received"
}

// Auction káº¿t thÃºc
{
  type: "AUCTION_ENDED",
  auctionId: 1,
  winner: "Bob",
  finalPrice: 30000000,
  totalBids: 25
}
```

## 8ï¸âƒ£ CÃ”NG NGHá»† NETWORK & PROTOCOL

### **A. HTTP/HTTPS (REST API)**
```
Protocol: HTTP/1.1
Method: GET, POST, PUT, DELETE
Format: JSON
Content-Type: application/json
Status Codes: 200, 201, 400, 401, 404, 500
```

### **B. WebSocket (Real-time)**
```
Protocol: WebSocket (ws:// hoáº·c wss://)
Sub-protocol: STOMP over SockJS
Message Format: JSON
Heartbeat: 10 seconds
```

**Táº¡i sao dÃ¹ng WebSocket?**
- âœ… **Hai chiá»u (bidirectional):** Server cÃ³ thá»ƒ push data xuá»‘ng client
- âœ… **Real-time:** Äá»™ trá»… tháº¥p (< 50ms)
- âœ… **Hiá»‡u quáº£:** 1 connection duy trÃ¬, khÃ´ng pháº£i poll liÃªn tá»¥c
- âœ… **PhÃ¹ há»£p Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡:** Cáº§n cáº­p nháº­t giÃ¡ ngay láº­p tá»©c

**So sÃ¡nh vá»›i alternatives:**
```
Long Polling:     KÃ©m hiá»‡u quáº£, nhiá»u HTTP requests
Server-Sent Events (SSE): Chá»‰ má»™t chiá»u (server â†’ client)
WebSocket:        âœ… Tá»‘t nháº¥t cho bidirectional real-time
```

---

## 9ï¸âƒ£ SECURITY (Báº£o máº­t)

### **Password Security**
```
Algorithm: BCrypt
Cost Factor: 12 rounds
Salt: Auto-generated per password
Storage: Chá»‰ lÆ°u hash, khÃ´ng lÆ°u plaintext
```

### **Session Management**
```
Method: HTTP Session (Spring Security)
Timeout: 30 minutes idle
Storage: In-memory (hoáº·c Redis náº¿u scale)
```

### **Input Validation**
```
Server-side validation:
- Annotation-based: @NotNull, @Min, @Max, @Email
- Custom validators
- SQL Injection prevention: JPA/Hibernate

Client-side validation:
- HTML5 validation attributes
- JavaScript validation
- Bootstrap form validation
```

### **HTTPS (Optional nhÆ°ng nÃªn cÃ³)**
```
Certificate: Let's Encrypt (free)
Protocol: TLS 1.3
Ports: 443 (HTTPS), 8443 (WebSocket Secure)
```

## 1ï¸âƒ£3ï¸âƒ£ ÄIá»‚M Ná»”I Báº¬T Vá»€ Láº¬P TRÃŒNH Máº NG (Cho Presentation)

### **1. Kiáº¿n trÃºc Client-Server â­â­â­â­â­**
```
- Web Browser (Client) â†” Spring Boot (Server) â†” MySQL
- RESTful API architecture
- Stateless HTTP requests
- Session-based authentication
```

### **2. Protocol Design â­â­â­â­â­**
```
HTTP/REST API:
- JSON format
- CRUD operations
- Status codes

WebSocket Protocol:
- STOMP messaging
- Pub/Sub pattern
- Real-time bidirectional communication
```

### **3. Real-time Communication â­â­â­â­â­**
```
WebSocket:
- Full-duplex communication
- Low latency (< 50ms)
- Server push notifications
- Broadcast to multiple clients
```

### **4. Concurrency Control â­â­â­â­**
```
JPA Optimistic Locking:
- @Version annotation
- Prevent race conditions
- Handle simultaneous bids

Synchronized methods:
- Thread-safe bid processing
```

### **5. Scalability â­â­â­**
```
Thread Pool:
- Spring Boot async execution
- Handle multiple concurrent users

Connection Pooling:
- HikariCP (default in Spring Boot)
- Efficient database connections
```

### **6. Security â­â­â­â­**
```
Spring Security:
- Authentication & Authorization
- BCrypt password hashing
- CSRF protection
- Session management
```

```plaintext
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
            â”‚
```

```plaintext
Columns:
- user_id (INT, PK, AUTO_INCREMENT)
- username (VARCHAR(50), UNIQUE, NOT NULL)
- email (VARCHAR(100), UNIQUE, NOT NULL)
- password_hash (VARCHAR(255), NOT NULL)
- full_name (VARCHAR(100))

- role (ENUM('USER', 'ADMIN'), DEFAULT 'USER')
- is_active (BOOLEAN, DEFAULT TRUE)
- created_at (TIMESTAMP, DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
- updated_at (TIMESTAMP, ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
```

```javascript
// Äáº·t giÃ¡
{
  type: "PLACE_BID",
  auctionId: 1,
  amount: 25000000
}

// Join auction room
{
  type: "JOIN_AUCTION",
  auctionId: 1
}

// Leave auction room
{
  type: "LEAVE_AUCTION",
  auctionId: 1
}
```

```javascript
// Cáº­p nháº­t giÃ¡ má»›i
{
  type: "BID_UPDATE",
  auctionId: 1,
  bidderName: "Bob",
  newPrice: 25000000,
  timeLeft: 145
}

// Báº¡n bá»‹ Ä‘Ã¨ giÃ¡
{
  type: "OUTBID_ALERT",
  auctionId: 1,
  newPrice: 26000000,
  newBidder: "Alice"
}

// Countdown tick
{
  type: "TIME_TICK",
  auctionId: 1,
  secondsLeft: 30
}

// Auction sáº¯p káº¿t thÃºc
{
  type: "AUCTION_ENDING_SOON",
  auctionId: 1,
  secondsLeft: 60
}

// Auction gia háº¡n
{
  type: "AUCTION_EXTENDED",
  auctionId: 1,
  newEndTime: "2025-10-28T15:05:00",
  reason: "Late bid received"
}

// Auction káº¿t thÃºc
{
  type: "AUCTION_ENDED",
  auctionId: 1,
  winner: "Bob",
  finalPrice: 30000000,
  totalBids: 25
}
```

```plaintext
Protocol: HTTP/1.1
Method: GET, POST, PUT, DELETE
Format: JSON
Content-Type: application/json
Status Codes: 200, 201, 400, 401, 404, 500
```

```plaintext
Protocol: WebSocket (ws:// hoáº·c wss://)
Sub-protocol: STOMP over SockJS
Message Format: JSON
Heartbeat: 10 seconds
```

```plaintext
Long Polling:     KÃ©m hiá»‡u quáº£, nhiá»u HTTP requests
Server-Sent Events (SSE): Chá»‰ má»™t chiá»u (server â†’ client)
WebSocket:        âœ… Tá»‘t nháº¥t cho bidirectional real-time
```

```plaintext
Algorithm: BCrypt
Cost Factor: 12 rounds
Salt: Auto-generated per password
Storage: Chá»‰ lÆ°u hash, khÃ´ng lÆ°u plaintext
```

```plaintext
Method: HTTP Session (Spring Security)
Timeout: 30 minutes idle
Storage: In-memory (hoáº·c Redis náº¿u scale)
```

```plaintext
Server-side validation:
- Annotation-based: @NotNull, @Min, @Max, @Email
- Custom validators
- SQL Injection prevention: JPA/Hibernate

Client-side validation:
- HTML5 validation attributes
- JavaScript validation
- Bootstrap form validation
```

```plaintext
Certificate: Let's Encrypt (free)
Protocol: TLS 1.3
Ports: 443 (HTTPS), 8443 (WebSocket Secure)
```

```properties
# Server
server.port=8080
spring.application.name=auction-system

# Database
spring.datasource.url=jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/auction_db?useSSL=false&serverTimezone=UTC
spring.datasource.username=root
spring.datasource.password=yourpassword
spring.datasource.driver-class-name=com.mysql.cj.jdbc.Driver

# JPA/Hibernate
spring.jpa.hibernate.ddl-auto=update
spring.jpa.show-sql=true
spring.jpa.properties.hibernate.dialect=org.hibernate.dialect.MySQL8Dialect
spring.jpa.properties.hibernate.format_sql=true

# Thymeleaf
spring.thymeleaf.cache=false
spring.thymeleaf.prefix=classpath:/templates/
spring.thymeleaf.suffix=.html

# File Upload (náº¿u upload áº£nh)
spring.servlet.multipart.max-file-size=5MB
spring.servlet.multipart.max-request-size=5MB

# Logging
logging.level.com.auction=DEBUG
logging.level.org.springframework.web=INFO
```

```xml
<dependencies>
    <!-- Spring Boot Starter Web -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-web</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Spring Boot WebSocket -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-websocket</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Spring Data JPA -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-data-jpa</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Spring Security -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-security</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Thymeleaf -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-thymeleaf</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Thymeleaf + Spring Security -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.thymeleaf.extras</groupId>
        <artifactId>thymeleaf-extras-springsecurity6</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- MySQL Driver -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>com.mysql</groupId>
        <artifactId>mysql-connector-j</artifactId>
        <scope>runtime</scope>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Lombok (optional - giáº£m boilerplate code) -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.projectlombok</groupId>
        <artifactId>lombok</artifactId>
        <optional>true</optional>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- Validation -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-validation</artifactId>
    </dependency>
    
    <!-- DevTools (auto-reload) -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-devtools</artifactId>
        <scope>runtime</scope>
        <optional>true</optional>
    </dependency>
</dependencies>
```

```plaintext
- Web Browser (Client) â†” Spring Boot (Server) â†” MySQL
- RESTful API architecture
- Stateless HTTP requests
- Session-based authentication
```

```plaintext
HTTP/REST API:
- JSON format
- CRUD operations
- Status codes

WebSocket Protocol:
- STOMP messaging
- Pub/Sub pattern
- Real-time bidirectional communication
```

```plaintext
WebSocket:
- Full-duplex communication
- Low latency (< 50ms)
- Server push notifications
- Broadcast to multiple clients
```

```plaintext
JPA Optimistic Locking:
- @Version annotation
- Prevent race conditions
- Handle simultaneous bids

Synchronized methods:
- Thread-safe bid processing
```

```plaintext
Thread Pool:
- Spring Boot async execution
- Handle multiple concurrent users

Connection Pooling:
- HikariCP (default in Spring Boot)
- Efficient database connections
```

```plaintext
Spring Security:
- Authentication & Authorization
- BCrypt password hashing
- CSRF protection
- Session management
```
